And of course, the parent may forward the same object to multiple children,\n     * and the child may forward it to grandchildren, etc. Therefore, you should be mindful\n     * of mutability.\n     * <p>\n     * The {@link Record} class itself is immutable (all the setter-style methods return an\n     * independent copy of the instance). However, the key, value, and headers referenced by\n     * the Record may themselves be mutable.\n     * <p>\n     * Some programs may opt to make use of this mutability for high performance, in which case\n     * the input record may be mutated and then forwarded by each {@link Processor}. However,\n     * most applications should instead favor safety.\n     * <p>\n     * Forwarding records safely simply means to make a copy of the record before you mutate it.\n     * This is trivial when using the {@link Record#withKey(Object)}, {@link Record#withValue(Object)},\n     * and {@link Record#withTimestamp(long)} methods, as each of these methods make a copy of the\n     * record as a matter of course. But a little extra care must be taken with headers, since\n     * the {@link org.apache.kafka.common.header.Header} class is mutable. The easiest way to\n     * safely handle headers is to use the {@link Record} constructors to make a copy before\n     * modifying headers.\n     * <p>\n     * In other words, this would be considered unsafe:\n     * <code>\n     *     process(Record inputRecord) {\n     *         inputRecord.headers().add(...);\n     *         context.forward(inputRecord);\n     *     }\n     * </code>\n     * This is unsafe because the parent, and potentially siblings, grandparents, etc.,\n     * all will see this modification to their shared Headers reference. This is a violation\n     * of causality and could lead to undefined behavior.\n     * <p>\n---\n/*\n * Licensed to the Apache Software Foundation (ASF) under one or more\n * contributor license agreements. See the NOTICE file distributed with\n * this work for additional information regarding copyright ownership.\n * The ASF licenses this file to You under the Apache License, Version 2.0\n * (the \"License\"); you may not use this file except in compliance with\n * the License. The `filter()` method uses `KTableFilter`; `mapValues()` uses `KTableMapValues`; `groupBy()` uses `KTableRepartitionMap` and returns `KGroupedTableImpl`.\\n- **KGroupedStreamImpl** (`streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KGroupedStreamImpl.java`): Implements `KGroupedStream` using `GroupedStreamAggregateBuilder` to build `KStreamAggregate`, `KStreamReduce`, and windowed aggregation processors.\\n- **KGroupedTableImpl** (`streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KGroupedTableImpl.java`): Implements `KGroupedTable` using `KTableAggregate` and `KTableReduce` processors.\\n\\n## Processor API Implementations for DSL Operations\\n\\n### map / mapValues\\n- **KStreamMap** (`streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamMap.java`): Implements `ProcessorSupplier` for `KStream.map()`. Used for key-changing operations (map, flatMap, groupBy).\\n- **FixedKeyProcessor** (`FixedKeyProcessor.java`): Interface for processors that do not change the key (mapValues, filter, filterNot).\\n- **ProcessorSupplier** (`ProcessorSupplier.java`): Factory interface for `Processor` instances, used by `KStream.process()`.\\n- **FixedKeyProcessorSupplier** (`FixedKeyProcessorSupplier.java`): Factory interface for `FixedKeyProcessor` instances, used by `KStream.processValues()`.\\n- **ContextualProcessor** (`ContextualProcessor.java`): Abstract base class managing `ProcessorContext` for processors.\\n- **ContextualFixedKeyProcessor** (`ContextualFixedKeyProcessor.java`): Abstract base class managing `FixedKeyProcessorContext` for fixed-key processors.\\n- **ProcessorContext** (`ProcessorContext.java`): Context for forwarding records and accessing state stores in key-changing processors.\\n- **FixedKeyProcessorContext** (`FixedKeyProcessorContext.java`): Context for fixed-key processors.\\n- **ProcessingContext** (`ProcessingContext.java`): Common base context interface.\\n- **Record** (`Record.java`): Immutable data class for records processed by `Processor`.\\n- **FixedKeyRecord** (`FixedKeyRecord.java`): Immutable data class for records processed by `FixedKeyProcessor`.\\n- **RecordMetadata** (`RecordMetadata.java`): Metadata about the record being processed.\\n\\n## Internal Interfaces\\n\\n- **KStreamAggProcessorSupplier** (`streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamAggProcessorSupplier.java`): Extends `ProcessorSupplier` for stream aggregation processors; adds `view()` and `enableSendingOldValues()`.\\n- **KTableProcessorSupplier** (`streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KTableProcessorSupplier.java`): Extends `ProcessorSupplier` for table processors; adds `view()` and `enableSendingOldValues()`.\\n- **KTableRepartitionMapSupplier** (`streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KTableRepartitionMapSupplier.java`): Extends `ProcessorSupplier` for table repartition map operations.\\n- **AbstractKStreamTimeWindowAggregateProcessor** (`streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/AbstractKStreamTimeWindowAggregateProcessor.java`): Abstract base class for time-window aggregation processors, extending `ContextualProcessor`.\\n\\n## Migration Pattern\\n\\nTo migrate from DSL to Processor API:\\n1. Replace `stream.map(mapper)` with `stream.process(new ProcessorSupplier<>() { ... })` using a custom `Processor` that calls `context().forward(record.withKey(...).withValue(...))`.\\n2. Replace `stream.filter(predicate)` with `stream.processValues(new FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<>() { ... })` using a `FixedKeyProcessor` that conditionally calls `context().forward(record)`.\\n3. Replace `stream.groupByKey().aggregate(...)` with a custom `Processor` that maintains a `KeyValueStore` state store, accessed via `context.getStateStore(storeName)`, and manually manages aggregation state.\"\n}\n",
